因为 $\boldsymbol{A}=(\boldsymbol{\alpha}_{1},\boldsymbol{\alpha}_{2},\boldsymbol{\alpha}_{3})\stackrel{r}{\sim}\boldsymbol{E}$ ，所以 $\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\alpha_{3}$ 是 $R^{3}$ 的一个基，且向量 $\boldsymbol{\beta}=\begin{pmatrix}2\\-1\\6\end{pmatrix}$ 在这组基下的坐标为 $\begin{pmatrix}7\\-2\\1\end{pmatrix}$ .

# 三、基变换与坐标变换

定义 6 设 $\alpha_{1}, \alpha_{2}, \cdots, \alpha_{n}$ 与 $\beta_{1}, \beta_{2}, \cdots, \beta_{n}$ 是 n 维向量空间 V 的两个基，存在系数矩阵 $P_{n \times n}$ ，使得

$$
\left(\boldsymbol {\beta} _ {1}, \boldsymbol {\beta} _ {2}, \dots , \boldsymbol {\beta} _ {n}\right) = \left(\boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {1}, \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {2}, \dots , \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {n}\right) \boldsymbol {P}.
$$

矩阵 $P_{n\times n}$ 称为从基 $\alpha_{1}, \alpha_{2}, \cdots, \alpha_{n}$ 到基 $\beta_{1}, \beta_{2}, \cdots, \beta_{n}$ 的过渡矩阵.

显然，从基 $\alpha_{1}, \alpha_{2}, \cdots, \alpha_{n}$ 到基 $\beta_{1}, \beta_{2}, \cdots, \beta_{n}$ 的过渡矩阵 $P_{n \times n}$ 是可逆矩阵.

例9 取定 $\mathbb{R}^3$ 中两组基 $\pmb{\alpha}_{1} = \begin{pmatrix} 1 \\ 1 \\ 0 \end{pmatrix}$ , $\pmb{\alpha}_{2} = \begin{pmatrix} 1 \\ 0 \\ 1 \end{pmatrix}$ , $\pmb{\alpha}_{3} = \begin{pmatrix} 0 \\ 1 \\ 1 \end{pmatrix}$ 和 $\pmb{\beta}_{1} = \begin{pmatrix} 1 \\ 1 \\ -2 \end{pmatrix}$ , $\pmb{\beta}_{2} = \begin{pmatrix} 1 \\ 2 \\ 3 \end{pmatrix}$ , $\pmb{\beta}_{3} = \begin{pmatrix} -1 \\ 2 \\ 1 \end{pmatrix}$ , 求从基 $\pmb{\alpha}_{1}, \pmb{\alpha}_{2}, \pmb{\alpha}_{3}$ 到基 $\pmb{\beta}_{1}, \pmb{\beta}_{2}, \pmb{\beta}_{3}$ 的过渡矩阵 $P$ .

解 记矩阵 $A=(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\alpha_{3})$ ， $B=(\beta_{1},\beta_{2},\beta_{3})$ ，则从自然基 $e_{1}$ ， $e_{2}$ ， $e_{3}$ 到基 $\alpha_{1}$ ， $\alpha_{2}$ ， $\alpha_{3}$ 的过渡矩阵就是 A，从基 $e_{1}$ ， $e_{2}$ ， $e_{3}$ 到基 $\beta_{1}$ ， $\beta_{2}$ ， $\beta_{3}$ 的过渡矩阵就是 B。于是有

$$
\left(\boldsymbol {\beta} _ {1}, \boldsymbol {\beta} _ {2}, \boldsymbol {\beta} _ {3}\right) = \left(\boldsymbol {e} _ {1}, \boldsymbol {e} _ {2}, \boldsymbol {e} _ {3}\right) \boldsymbol {B} = \left(\boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {1}, \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {2}, \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {3}\right) \boldsymbol {A} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {B}.
$$

记 $P=A^{-1}B$ ，则矩阵 P 就是从基 $\alpha_{1}, \alpha_{2}, \alpha_{3}$ 到基 $\beta_{1}, \beta_{2}, \beta_{3}$ 的过渡矩阵.

$$
(\boldsymbol {A} \mid \boldsymbol {B}) = \left(\begin{array}{c c c c c c}1&1&0&1&1&- 1\\1&0&1&1&2&2\\0&1&1&- 2&3&1\end{array}\right)\rightarrow \left(\begin{array}{c c c c c c}1&0&0&2&0&0\\0&1&0&- 1&1&- 1\\0&0&1&- 1&2&2\end{array}\right),
$$

因此

$$
\boldsymbol {P} = \boldsymbol {A} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {B} = \left( \begin{array}{c c c} 2 & 0 & 0 \\ - 1 & 1 & - 1 \\ - 1 & 2 & 2 \end{array} \right).
$$

设 $\alpha_{1}, \alpha_{2}, \cdots, \alpha_{n}$ 与 $\beta_{1}, \beta_{2}, \cdots, \beta_{n}$ 是 $R^{n}$ 的两个基，任一向量 $\alpha \in R^{n}$ 在基 $\alpha_{1}, \alpha_{2}, \cdots, \alpha_{n}$ 与基 $\beta_{1}, \beta_{2}, \cdots, \beta_{n}$ 下的坐标分别为 $(x_{1}, x_{2}, \cdots, x_{n})^{\mathrm{T}}$ 和 $(y_{1}, y_{2}, \cdots, y_{n})^{\mathrm{T}}$ ，即

$$
\boldsymbol {\alpha} = \left(\boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {1}, \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {2}, \dots , \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {n}\right) \left( \begin{array}{c} x _ {1} \\ x _ {2} \\ \vdots \\ x _ {n} \end{array} \right), \boldsymbol {\alpha} = \left(\boldsymbol {\beta} _ {1}, \boldsymbol {\beta} _ {2}, \dots , \boldsymbol {\beta} _ {n}\right) \left( \begin{array}{c} y _ {1} \\ y _ {2} \\ \vdots \\ y _ {n} \end{array} \right).
$$

令矩阵 $\boldsymbol{A}=(\boldsymbol{\alpha}_{1},\boldsymbol{\alpha}_{2},\cdots,\boldsymbol{\alpha}_{n})$ ， $\boldsymbol{B}=(\boldsymbol{\beta}_{1},\boldsymbol{\beta}_{2},\cdots,\boldsymbol{\beta}_{n})$ ，则有

$$
\boldsymbol {A} \left( \begin{array}{c} x _ {1} \\ x _ {2} \\ \vdots \\ x _ {n} \end{array} \right) = \boldsymbol {B} \left( \begin{array}{c} y _ {1} \\ y _ {2} \\ \vdots \\ y _ {n} \end{array} \right).
$$

于是得到

$$
\left( \begin{array}{c} x _ {1} \\ x _ {2} \\ \vdots \\ x _ {n} \end{array} \right) = \boldsymbol {A} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {B} \left( \begin{array}{c} y _ {1} \\ y _ {2} \\ \vdots \\ y _ {n} \end{array} \right) = \boldsymbol {P} \left( \begin{array}{c} y _ {1} \\ y _ {2} \\ \vdots \\ y _ {n} \end{array} \right) \tag {5-1}
$$

或

$$
\left( \begin{array}{c} y _ {1} \\ y _ {2} \\ \vdots \\ y _ {n} \end{array} \right) = \boldsymbol {B} ^ {- 1} \boldsymbol {A} \left( \begin{array}{c} x _ {1} \\ x _ {2} \\ \vdots \\ x _ {n} \end{array} \right) = \boldsymbol {P} ^ {- 1} \left( \begin{array}{c} x _ {1} \\ x _ {2} \\ \vdots \\ x _ {n} \end{array} \right). \tag {5-2}
$$

其中 $P=A^{-1}B$ 是从基 $\alpha_{1}, \alpha_{2}, \cdots, \alpha_{n}$ 到基 $\beta_{1}, \beta_{2}, \cdots, \beta_{n}$ 的过渡矩阵.

定义 7 式(5-1)称为从坐标 $(y_{1}, y_{2}, \cdots, y_{n})^{\mathrm{T}}$ 到坐标 $(x_{1}, x_{2}, \cdots, x_{n})^{\mathrm{T}}$ 的坐标变换公式；式(5-2)称为从坐标 $(x_{1}, x_{2}, \cdots, x_{n})^{\mathrm{T}}$ 到坐标 $(y_{1}, y_{2}, \cdots, y_{n})^{\mathrm{T}}$ 的坐标变换公式.

例10 已知向量 $\pmb{\alpha} \in \mathbb{R}^3$ 在基 $\pmb{\alpha}_1 = \begin{pmatrix} 1 \\ 1 \\ 0 \end{pmatrix}$ , $\pmb{\alpha}_2 = \begin{pmatrix} 1 \\ 0 \\ 1 \end{pmatrix}$ , $\pmb{\alpha}_3 = \begin{pmatrix} 0 \\ 1 \\ 1 \end{pmatrix}$ 下的坐标是 $\begin{pmatrix} 8 \\ -2 \\ 4 \end{pmatrix}$ , 求 $\pmb{\alpha}$ 在基 $\pmb{\beta}_1 = \begin{pmatrix} 1 \\ 1 \\ -2 \end{pmatrix}$ , $\pmb{\beta}_2 = \begin{pmatrix} 1 \\ 2 \\ 3 \end{pmatrix}$ , $\pmb{\beta}_3 = \begin{pmatrix} -1 \\ 2 \\ 1 \end{pmatrix}$ 下的坐标.

解 设 $\alpha$ 在基 $\beta_{1}, \beta_{2}, \beta_{3}$ 下的坐标为 $(y_{1}, y_{2}, y_{3})^{\mathrm{T}}$ ，由例 9 知，从基 $\alpha_{1}, \alpha_{2}, \alpha_{3}$ 

到基 $\pmb{\beta}_{1}$ ， $\pmb{\beta}_{2}$ ， $\pmb{\beta}_{3}$ 的过渡矩阵为 $P = \begin{pmatrix} 2 & 0 & 0\\ -1 & 1 & -1\\ -1 & 2 & 2 \end{pmatrix}$ ，易求得 $P^{-1} = \left( \begin{array}{ccc}\frac{1}{2} & 0 & 0\\ \frac{3}{8} & \frac{1}{2} & \frac{1}{4}\\ -\frac{1}{8} & -\frac{1}{2} & \frac{1}{4} \end{array} \right)$ ，于是由

式(5-2)有

$$
\left( \begin{array}{l} y _ {1} \\ y _ {2} \\ y _ {3} \end{array} \right) = \boldsymbol {P} ^ {- 1} \left( \begin{array}{l} x _ {1} \\ x _ {2} \\ x _ {3} \end{array} \right) = \left( \begin{array}{c c c} \frac {1}{2} & 0 & 0 \\ \frac {3}{8} & \frac {1}{2} & \frac {1}{4} \\ - \frac {1}{8} & - \frac {1}{2} & \frac {1}{4} \end{array} \right) \left( \begin{array}{l} 8 \\ - 2 \\ 4 \end{array} \right) = \left( \begin{array}{l} 4 \\ 3 \\ 1 \end{array} \right).
$$

# 习题3-5

1. 判断下列集合对通常的向量加法和数乘运算是否构成向量空间，并说明理由：

(1) $V_{1}=\left\{\boldsymbol{x}=\left(x_{1},x_{2},\cdots,x_{n}\right)^{\mathrm{T}}\mid x_{1},\cdots,x_{n}\in\mathbb{R}\text{且满足}x_{1}+\cdots+x_{n}=0\right\};$ 

(2) $V_{2}=\left\{\boldsymbol{x}=\left(x_{1},x_{2},\cdots,x_{n}\right)^{\mathrm{T}}\mid x_{1},\cdots,x_{n}\in\mathbb{R}\text{且满足}x_{1}+\cdots+x_{n}=1\right\};$ 

(3) $V_{3}=\left\{\boldsymbol{x}=\left(x_{1},x_{2},\cdots,x_{n}\right)^{\mathrm{T}}\mid x_{1},\cdots,x_{n}\in\mathbb{R}\text{且}x_{1}=x_{2}=\cdots=x_{n}\right\}.$ 

2. 设向量组 $\alpha_{1}, \alpha_{2}, \cdots, \alpha_{s}$ 与向量组 $\beta_{1}, \beta_{2}, \cdots, \beta_{t}$ 等价，记

$$
\mathfrak {L} _ {1} \left(\boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {1}, \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {2}, \dots , \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {s}\right) = \left\{\boldsymbol {\alpha} = k _ {1} \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {1} + k _ {2} \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {2} + \dots + k _ {s} \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {s} \mid k _ {1}, k _ {2}, \dots , k _ {s} \in \mathbb {R} \right\},
$$

$$
\mathfrak {L} _ {2} \left(\boldsymbol {\beta} _ {1}, \boldsymbol {\beta} _ {2}, \dots , \boldsymbol {\beta} _ {t}\right) = \left\{\boldsymbol {\beta} = k _ {1} \boldsymbol {\beta} _ {1} + k _ {2} \boldsymbol {\beta} _ {2} + \dots + k _ {t} \boldsymbol {\beta} _ {t} \mid k _ {1}, k _ {2}, \dots , k _ {t} \in \mathbb {R} \right\},
$$

证明： $\mathfrak{L}(\boldsymbol{\alpha}_{1},\boldsymbol{\alpha}_{2},\cdots,\boldsymbol{\alpha}_{s})=\mathfrak{L}_{2}(\boldsymbol{\beta}_{1},\boldsymbol{\beta}_{2},\cdots,\boldsymbol{\beta}_{t}).$ 

3. 设向量组

$$
\boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {1} = \left( \begin{array}{c} 1 \\ 2 \\ 3 \\ - 1 \end{array} \right), \quad \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {2} = \left( \begin{array}{c} 2 \\ 2 \\ 2 \\ - 1 \end{array} \right), \quad \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {3} = \left( \begin{array}{c} 2 \\ 3 \\ 1 \\ 1 \end{array} \right), \quad \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {4} = \left( \begin{array}{c} 3 \\ 2 \\ 1 \\ - 1 \end{array} \right), \quad \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {5} = \left( \begin{array}{c} - 1 \\ - 1 \\ 2 \\ - 2 \end{array} \right),
$$

求向量空间 $\mathfrak{L}(\pmb{\alpha}_1, \pmb{\alpha}_2, \pmb{\alpha}_3, \pmb{\alpha}_4, \pmb{\alpha}_5) = \{\pmb{\alpha} = k_1\pmb{\alpha}_1 + k_2\pmb{\alpha}_2 + k_3\pmb{\alpha}_3 + k_4\pmb{\alpha}_4 + k_5\pmb{\alpha}_5 | k_1, k_2, k_3, k_4, k_5 \in \mathbb{R}\}$ 的基与维数.

4. 验证

(1) 

$$
\boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {1} = \left( \begin{array}{c} 1 \\ 0 \\ 0 \\ 0 \end{array} \right), \quad \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {2} = \left( \begin{array}{c} 1 \\ 1 \\ 0 \\ 0 \end{array} \right), \quad \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {3} = \left( \begin{array}{c} 1 \\ 1 \\ 1 \\ 0 \end{array} \right), \quad \boldsymbol {\alpha} _ {4} = \left( \begin{array}{c} 1 \\ 1 \\ 1 \\ 1 \end{array} \right)
$$

是 $R^{4}$ 的一个基，并求 $\boldsymbol{\alpha}=(1,1,2,1)^{T}$ 在这个基下的坐标.

(2) 

$$
\boldsymbol {\beta} _ {1} = \left( \begin{array}{c} 1 \\ 0 \\ 1 \\ 1 \end{array} \right), \boldsymbol {\beta} _ {2} = \left( \begin{array}{c} 1 \\ 1 \\ 0 \\ 1 \end{array} \right), \boldsymbol {\beta} _ {3} = \left( \begin{array}{c} 1 \\ 1 \\ 1 \\ 0 \end{array} \right), \boldsymbol {\beta} _ {4} = \left( \begin{array}{c} 0 \\ 1 \\ 1 \\ 1 \end{array} \right)
$$

也是 $\mathbb{R}^4$ 的一个基，并求从基 $\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\alpha_{3},\alpha_{4}$ 到基 $\beta_{1},\beta_{2},\beta_{3},\beta_{4}$ 的过渡矩阵 $P$ ，以及 $\pmb {\alpha} = (1,1,2,1)^{\mathrm{T}}$ 在基 $\beta_{1},\beta_{2},\beta_{3},\beta_{4}$ 下的坐标.

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-05-14/af9e42fb-2909-4662-af4d-d5e75a74eb9d/bb4ddf74b7a1719826cfc617e3120e0789043dd3acc27ce0bf9fe711d4a69272.jpg)
